<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1c276855-85f7-450d-abd4-9bb2e9f1576b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer2015423314993302583">In a long forgotten time a terrible war raged, entire countries were razed and even magic itself was decimated.   <span id="freeText2015423314993302583" style="display:none">In a long forgotten time a terrible war raged, entire countries were razed and even magic itself was decimated. According to myth the only survivors were Immortals, powerful sorcerers who achieved life everlasting. With the fall of the old world they scattered to the wild frontiers, or so the tale goes. Time marches on however and with magic barely an echo of its former self, technology presses on. The rising nation of The Syndicate is at the forefront making breakthrough after breakthrough in a handful of years. Establishing bases in the far flung frontier regions they have started a new endeavour of research into the ancient world, heedless of cost or consequence. As The Syndicate pushes deeper into the wilderness spurred on by ambition, mysterious deaths follow. Is this just the dangers of the wild, the resistance of the local tribes, or something else awoken by this intrusion?</span>

<div id="review_2366332841" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2366332841" />
    <a title="Our Book Club" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67636305-our-book-club"><img alt="Our Book Club" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494340330p2/67636305.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2366332841?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Our Book Club" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Our Book Club" href="/user/show/67636305-our-book-club">Our Book Club</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2366332841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5071719213487044175">If you are looking for an E-book that will entertain you for the time being, that has a retro feeling to it, try this gem out! It started off slowly but eventually became fast-paced as I got to the middle of it with the characters and plot having a Star Wars meets Conan the Barbarian edge that will cause the nostalgic in you to call it a favorite for the moment. The focus is on two areas called the Low and the government-esque Syndicate who is venturing into the Low to claim it and for purposes </span>
  <span id="freeText5071719213487044175" style="display:none">If you are looking for an E-book that will entertain you for the time being, that has a retro feeling to it, try this gem out! It started off slowly but eventually became fast-paced as I got to the middle of it with the characters and plot having a Star Wars meets Conan the Barbarian edge that will cause the nostalgic in you to call it a favorite for the moment. The focus is on two areas called the Low and the government-esque Syndicate who is venturing into the Low to claim it and for purposes that have to do with researching the magical elements that the Low is known for.<br /><br />This story has a lot of characters and the main ones I think are the sorcerer titled Old Owl, the dark-haired siblings Maeca and Boan, Rima the matriarch of the tribe of Ursan Mao that settled in the Low after Old Owl put an end to their capturers, Neira the Syndicate’s fierce and vicious researcher, and Commanders Kaul, Finn, and Trate. They all come face to face with the bloodthirsty monsters known as the Kran who are half ant and half primate who seem to feed on the impact of their weapons and magic instead of diminishing under them.<br /><br />I urge you the bookworm to try this one out and see if it will enthrall you as it has done to me. Please disregard of the unexciting front cover image (if you are not into retro and the 70s or 80s) because the story is astonishingly addictive. I could not put it down when the battle started. I can see it being made into an action-packed motion picture like the ones I mentioned early on in this review because the writing is good, the lines of the characters are superb, and the pacing is excellent. I will not reveal further details about this book because that will spoil its appeal. I recommend it to all fans of the Sci-Fi channel and to those who grew up in the 80’s on films like Krull, Star Wars, and Conan the Barbarian. My overall favorite character in this book is Red Rabbit who appeared later for her aesthetics and grueling dislike for an equally vicious female character. Find out about their feud and more when you buy this book today! Enjoy!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5071719213487044175" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2318693504" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2318693504" />
    <a title="My World of Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/78838161-my-world-of-reviews"><img alt="My World of Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520362273p2/78838161.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2318693504?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="My World of Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="My World of Reviews" href="/user/show/78838161-my-world-of-reviews">My World of Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2318693504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7356408257244241324">Coming Storm by David J. Morden is a great example of simple and pure science fiction. It almost has a retro vibe making it appealing to a lot of different people, old and young alike. A fantasy, dystopian novel really geared toward the YA audience, the writing is good enough for adults as well. With a vast history of wars and destruction, this novel begins on tenuous ground, times are tough. The Syndicate is a rising nation on the threshold of taking over many lands with their technological end</span>
  <span id="freeText7356408257244241324" style="display:none">Coming Storm by David J. Morden is a great example of simple and pure science fiction. It almost has a retro vibe making it appealing to a lot of different people, old and young alike. A fantasy, dystopian novel really geared toward the YA audience, the writing is good enough for adults as well. With a vast history of wars and destruction, this novel begins on tenuous ground, times are tough. The Syndicate is a rising nation on the threshold of taking over many lands with their technological endeavors. The Syndicate is investigating a specific section called the Low, which in the past had magical powers. The Syndicate wants to claim these mysterious powers for themselves, and will go to extreme lengths to harness them. There are a lot of characters to keep track of, but they are fairly well drawn and work well and cohesively in the story. The plot moves forward nicely with a bit of tension to keep it interesting. Highly recommend for a fantastical read that reminds one of classic science fiction.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7356408257244241324" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2427635325" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2427635325" />
    <a title="Absolute Lit" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/73013126-absolute-lit"><img alt="Absolute Lit" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529313499p2/73013126.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2427635325?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2427635325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1531363777986945082">Fans of Space Operas, like those written by the likes of the great Iain Banks and Peter F. Hamilton, are sure to enjoy Coming Storm by David J Morden. Lots of interesting characters, plot the intertwine and weave together, and an epic battle that will decide the fate of an entire planet. What more can you want from a Science Fiction novel? Morden's writing is detailed, building up a background to the world he has created, to create a piece of fiction that is substantial, engaging, convincing and</span>
  <span id="freeText1531363777986945082" style="display:none">Fans of Space Operas, like those written by the likes of the great Iain Banks and Peter F. Hamilton, are sure to enjoy Coming Storm by David J Morden. Lots of interesting characters, plot the intertwine and weave together, and an epic battle that will decide the fate of an entire planet. What more can you want from a Science Fiction novel? Morden's writing is detailed, building up a background to the world he has created, to create a piece of fiction that is substantial, engaging, convincing and captivating. <br /><br />In a dystopian future, the Syndicate plays the role of government, advancing technology, creating infrastructure, and apparently 'researching' distant lands- known as the Low - for the future. But, the Syndicate has an ulterior motive for this research, and even deaths of their people will not quell their ambition. What have they disturbed in these wild and ancient lands? And what will the consequences be?<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1531363777986945082" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2460057218" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2460057218" />
    <a title="Profundito" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/84279706-profundito"><img alt="Profundito" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531831137p2/84279706.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2460057218?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Profundito" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Profundito" href="/user/show/84279706-profundito">Profundito</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2460057218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2326998633909657994">'Coming Storm' by David J Morden takes place in the far future, where the wars of the past are long forgotten, and the new power of the Syndicate forges forward. Wary of the threats that exist within the remnants of the ancient world, the Syndicate explores further and further flung regions, determined to claim what magical powers remain for themselves, to add to their advanced technology and weaponry. There is nothing the Syndicate won't do to remain the dominant power, but those residing in th</span>
  <span id="freeText2326998633909657994" style="display:none">'Coming Storm' by David J Morden takes place in the far future, where the wars of the past are long forgotten, and the new power of the Syndicate forges forward. Wary of the threats that exist within the remnants of the ancient world, the Syndicate explores further and further flung regions, determined to claim what magical powers remain for themselves, to add to their advanced technology and weaponry. There is nothing the Syndicate won't do to remain the dominant power, but those residing in the 'Low' will not be oppressed so easily...prepare for war!!<br /><br />What I really loved about 'Coming Storm' was its homage to vintage Sci-Fi, reminiscent of the brilliant 'Dune' franchise by Frank Herbert. Something that is gritty and a little dark, but with plenty of action, a unique plot, and of course, good vs. evil. This is a must-read for fans of Science Fiction, particularly of the golden age of the 1970's, I can't wait to read more from David J Morden in the future.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2326998633909657994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2423716682" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2423716682" />
    <a title="Chapter Adapter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72888963-chapter-adapter"><img alt="Chapter Adapter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528979376p2/72888963.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2423716682?book_show_action=true">Jun 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chapter Adapter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chapter Adapter" href="/user/show/72888963-chapter-adapter">Chapter Adapter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2423716682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer868743574803133164">This is old-school sci-fi at its very best. I’m not so much a fan of science fiction these days but this is a throwback to some of the classics I loved while growing up. You aren’t thrown in the deep end of action as you first begin reading as there are some important revelations and world-building necessary first. And once things get going they really get going. <br/><br/>The writing is really quite compelling but doesn’t make unnecessary technical complications like some sci-fi authors feel the need to </span>
  <span id="freeText868743574803133164" style="display:none">This is old-school sci-fi at its very best. I’m not so much a fan of science fiction these days but this is a throwback to some of the classics I loved while growing up. You aren’t thrown in the deep end of action as you first begin reading as there are some important revelations and world-building necessary first. And once things get going they really get going. <br /><br />The writing is really quite compelling but doesn’t make unnecessary technical complications like some sci-fi authors feel the need to do. Morden lets the characters and plot do that work and the book is all the much stronger for it. I’m now a fan and I’ll be back for more Morden.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="868743574803133164" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bxxbF3R7j1eSDI9jRZfxOHmVWYL1j68mRVyrwRW1PsOFzfHz6U8iNcAYc5HPOAstfm5OEyQkSyYiDRwKz5eB5A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

As Chief of Surgical Oncology at Baylor College of Medicine, Dr. Steven Curley has worked with cancer patients for over two decades. While his life\'s work has been to help his patients live longer lives, he found that they helped him in ways he never could have expected. IN MY HANDS is a rare, often emotional look at some of Dr. Curley\'s real patients and real situations in modern cancer care. These stories of resilience, hope, and determination changed and inspired Dr. Curley, and he uses these same stories to encourage patients dealing with the fear and uncertainty coupled with a diagnosis of cancer. Every story in the book has a theme inspired by his patients: Hope, Courage, Strength, Determination, Wonder, Cooperation, Creativity, Diligence, Service, Perseverance, Wisdom, Grace, Consideration, Gratitude, Discernment, Reverence, Resourcefulness, Faith, Beauty, Acceptance, and Empathy. Some are positive messages, reminding us of the importance of maintaining balance between family, work, and leisure activities. Others are examples of the remarkable resilience of the human spirit when facing the reality of and the surgical risks that accompany a cancer diagnosis. Realistically, despite remarkable advances in multidisciplinary cancer care, some remind us cancer is still a potentially lethal and destructive disease affecting patients and the family and friends supporting them. While many people are told that there is no hope in their situation, Dr. Curley\'s patients taught him to always provide hope, to push the envelope and give people a chance, and that hope is a critical component of treatment and care. Finding Hope in the Darkness of Grief is a gleaning of insights from artist Diamante Lavender. For her, life has been a long, difficult road, but it has taught many poignant lessons. Her poetry collection is an exploration of the human soul, a traversing of situations that life throws at us. Diamante has always been intrigued by the ability to overcome and move on to bigger and better things. She writes to encourage hope and possibility in those who read her stories.
